\end{DoxyCompactItemize}


\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
The \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine}{I\+Rtc\+Engine}} class.

This class provides the main methods that can be invoked by your app.

\mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine}{I\+Rtc\+Engine}} is the basic interface class of the Agora Native S\+DK. Creating an \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine}{I\+Rtc\+Engine}} object and then calling the methods of this object enables you to use Agora Native S\+DK\textquotesingle{}s communication functionality. 

\doxysubsection{Member Function Documentation}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_afe4804c1f53bfee301c0960fda006c47}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_afe4804c1f53bfee301c0960fda006c47}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!release@{release}}
\index{release@{release}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{release()}{release()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual void agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::release (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{sync = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Releases the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine}{I\+Rtc\+Engine}} object.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sync} & Determines whether this method is a synchronous call.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: This method is a synchronous call, which means that the result of this method call returns after the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine}{I\+Rtc\+Engine}} object resources are released. Do not call this method in any callback generated by the S\+DK, or it may result in a deadlock. The S\+DK automatically detects the deadlock and turns this method into an asynchronous call, but the test itself takes extra time.
\item false\+: This method is an asynchronous call. The result returns immediately even when the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine}{I\+Rtc\+Engine}} object resources are not released.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Do not immediately uninstall the S\+DK\textquotesingle{}s dynamic library after the call, or it may crash because the S\+DK clean-\/up thread has not quit.
\item Call this method in the sub-\/thread.
\item Once the app destroys the created \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine}{I\+Rtc\+Engine}} instance, you cannot use any method or callback in the S\+DK. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac71db65e66942e4e0a0550e95c16890f}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac71db65e66942e4e0a0550e95c16890f}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!initialize@{initialize}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{initialize()}{initialize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::initialize (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_rtc_engine_context}{Rtc\+Engine\+Context}} \&}]{context }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Initializes the Agora S\+DK service.

In this method, you need to enter the issued Agora App ID to start initialization. After creating an \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine}{I\+Rtc\+Engine}} object, call this method to initialize the service before calling any other methods. After the initialization, the service is set to enable audio by default.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_adc937172e59bd2695ea171553a88188c}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_adc937172e59bd2695ea171553a88188c}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!joinChannel@{joinChannel}}
\index{joinChannel@{joinChannel}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{joinChannel()}{joinChannel()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::join\+Channel (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{token,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{channel\+Id,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{info,  }\item[{uid\+\_\+t}]{uid }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Joins a channel.

Users in the same channel can talk to each other; and multiple users in the same channel can start a group chat. Note that users using different App I\+Ds cannot call each other.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This method allows you to join only one channel at a time.
\item A channel does not accept duplicate {\ttfamily uid}s, that is, two users with the same uid. If you set {\ttfamily uid} as 0, the system automatically assigns a user ID.
\item Ensure that the app ID you use to generate the token is the same app ID that you pass in the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac71db65e66942e4e0a0550e95c16890f}{initialize}} method.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em token} & The token for authentication.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item In situations not requiring high security\+: You can use the temporary token generated at Console. For details, see \href{https://docs.agora.io/en/Agora\%20Platform/token?platform=All\%20Platforms\#get-a-temporary-token}{\texttt{ Get a temporary token}}.
\item In situations requiring high security\+: Set it as the token generated at you server. For details, see \href{https://docs.agora.io/en/Agora\%20Platform/token?platform=All\%20Platforms\#get-a-token}{\texttt{ Generate a token}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em channel\+Id} & The unique channel name for the Agora\+R\+TC session in the string format. The string length must be less than 64 bytes. Supported character scopes are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item All lowercase English letters\+: a to z.
\item All uppercase English letters\+: A to Z.
\item All numeric characters\+: 0 to 9.
\item The space character.
\item Punctuation characters and other symbols, including\+: \char`\"{}!\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\#\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\%\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\&\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}(\char`\"{}, \char`\"{})\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}+\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}-\/\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+:\char`\"{}, \char`\"{};\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$<$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}=\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}.\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$>$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}?\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}@\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\mbox{[}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\mbox{]}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$^\wedge$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\+\_\+\char`\"{}, \char`\"{} \{\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}\}\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$\vert$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}$\sim$\char`\"{}, \char`\"{},\char`\"{}. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em info} & (\mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1_optional}{Optional}}) Additional information about the channel that you want to add. It can be set as a N\+U\+LL string or channel related information. Other users in the channel will not receive this message. \\
\hline
{\em uid} & (\mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1_optional}{Optional}}) User ID\+: A 32-\/bit unsigned integer ranging from 1 to (2$^\wedge$32-\/1). It must be unique. If not assigned (or set to 0), the S\+DK assigns one and reports it in the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_aafceb1f91ae9bd82317bf25981e6851b}{on\+Join\+Channel\+Success}} callback. Your app must record and maintain the returned value as the S\+DK does not maintain it.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a51c12d209373650638bfd82e28777081}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a51c12d209373650638bfd82e28777081}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!leaveChannel@{leaveChannel}}
\index{leaveChannel@{leaveChannel}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{leaveChannel()}{leaveChannel()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::leave\+Channel (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Leaves the channel.

This method allows a user to leave the channel, for example, by hanging up or exiting a call.

This method is an asynchronous call, which means that the result of this method returns even before the user has not actually left the channel. Once the user successfully leaves the channel, the S\+DK triggers the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a98f832d175dfc044b31f0ec5874460fb}{on\+Leave\+Channel}} callback.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If you call \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_afe4804c1f53bfee301c0960fda006c47}{release}} immediately after this method, the leave\+Channel process will be interrupted, and the S\+DK will not trigger the {\ttfamily on\+Leave\+Channel} callback.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ad5c2ef631e3e4076f6aec96ed1152262}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ad5c2ef631e3e4076f6aec96ed1152262}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!leaveChannel@{leaveChannel}}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a8f25b5ff97e2a070a69102e379295739}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a8f25b5ff97e2a070a69102e379295739}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!renewToken@{renewToken}}
\index{renewToken@{renewToken}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{renewToken()}{renewToken()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::renew\+Token (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{token }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Renews the token.

Once a token is enabled and used, it expires after a certain period of time.

Under the following circumstances, generate a new token on your server, and then call this method to renew it. Failure to do so results in the S\+DK disconnecting from the server.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler}{I\+Rtc\+Engine\+Event\+Handler}} on\+Token\+Privilege\+Will\+Expire \char`\"{}on\+Token\+Privilege\+Will\+Expire\char`\"{} callback is triggered;
\item The \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_aa7b456b750f56ca8fdfee8611572310e}{on\+Request\+Token}} callback is triggered;
\item The {\ttfamily E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+T\+O\+K\+E\+N\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+I\+R\+ED(-\/109)} error is reported.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em token} & The new token. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_aab53788c74da25080bad61f0525d12ae}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_aab53788c74da25080bad61f0525d12ae}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setChannelProfile@{setChannelProfile}}
\index{setChannelProfile@{setChannelProfile}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setChannelProfile()}{setChannelProfile()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Channel\+Profile (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{C\+H\+A\+N\+N\+E\+L\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}]{profile }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets the channel profile.

The \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine}{I\+Rtc\+Engine}} differentiates channel profiles and applies different optimization algorithms accordingly. For example, it prioritizes smoothness and low latency for a video call, and prioritizes video quality for a video broadcast.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item To ensure the quality of real-\/time communication, we recommend that all users in a channel use the same channel profile.
\item Call this method before calling {\ttfamily join\+Channel}. You cannot set the channel profile once you have joined the channel.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em profile} & The channel profile\+: \#\+C\+H\+A\+N\+N\+E\+L\+\_\+\+P\+R\+O\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a89ca6a15d5a388f3c82038e74bad4040}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a89ca6a15d5a388f3c82038e74bad4040}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setClientRole@{setClientRole}}
\index{setClientRole@{setClientRole}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setClientRole()}{setClientRole()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Client\+Role (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{C\+L\+I\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+O\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}]{role }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets the role of a user.

This method sets the user role as either B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+ER or A\+U\+D\+I\+E\+N\+CE (default).
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The broadcaster sends and receives streams.
\item The audience receives streams only.
\end{DoxyItemize}

By default, all users are audience regardless of the channel profile. Call this method to change the user role to B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+ER so that the user can send a stream.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
After calling the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a89ca6a15d5a388f3c82038e74bad4040}{set\+Client\+Role()}} method to C\+L\+I\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+O\+L\+E\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+E\+N\+CE, the S\+DK stops audio recording. However, C\+L\+I\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+O\+L\+E\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+E\+N\+CE will keep audio recording with A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+S\+C\+E\+N\+A\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+C\+H\+A\+T\+R\+O\+O\+M(5). Normally, app developer can also use mute api to achieve the same result, and we implement this \textquotesingle{}non-\/orthogonal\textquotesingle{} behavior only to make A\+PI backward compatible.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em role} & The role of the client\+: \#\+C\+L\+I\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+O\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{setClientRole@{setClientRole}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setClientRole()}{setClientRole()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Client\+Role (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{C\+L\+I\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+O\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}]{role,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_client_role_options}{Client\+Role\+Options}} \&}]{options }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets the role of the user, such as a host or an audience (default), before joining a channel in the live interactive streaming.

This method can be used to switch the user role in the live interactive streaming after the user joins a channel.

In the {\ttfamily L\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+I\+NG} profile, when a user switches user roles after joining a channel, a successful \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a89ca6a15d5a388f3c82038e74bad4040}{set\+Client\+Role}} method call triggers the following callbacks\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The local client\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a36d3f45184cbb37ed2c4846654a14368}{on\+Client\+Role\+Changed}}
\item The remote client\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a985a675469baf9d54feb8781732e0ca8}{on\+User\+Joined}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a9602593c05a16eafa7c094aa330c0719}{on\+User\+Offline}} (B\+E\+C\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+E\+N\+CE)
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This method applies only to the {\ttfamily L\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+I\+NG} profile.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em role} & Sets the role of the user. See \#\+C\+L\+I\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+O\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE. \\

{\em options} & Sets the audience latency level of the user. See \#\+Client\+Role\+Options.\\
\hline

\item $<$ 0\+: Failure.

\item -\/2(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+A\+L\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+R\+G\+U\+M\+E\+NT)\+: The parameter is invalid.
\item -\/7(E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+I\+N\+I\+T\+I\+A\+L\+I\+Z\+ED)\+: The S\+DK is not initialized.

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!startEchoTest@{startEchoTest}}
\index{startEchoTest@{startEchoTest}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{startEchoTest()}{startEchoTest()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::start\+Echo\+Test (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Starts an audio call test.

This method launches an audio call test to determine whether the audio devices (for example, headset and speaker) and the network connection are working properly.

In the test, the user first speaks, and the recording is played back in 10 seconds. If the user can hear the recording in 10 seconds, it indicates that the audio devices and network connection work properly.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
After calling the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac6b66af7fafbddae9f5dd85fe43ae879}{start\+Echo\+Test()}} method, always call \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ae779da1c3fe153d73e8dfb2eb59ba9e4}{stop\+Echo\+Test()}} to end the test. Otherwise, the app cannot run the next echo test, nor can it call the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_adc937172e59bd2695ea171553a88188c}{join\+Channel()}} method.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a842ed126b6e21a39059adaa4caa6d021}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a842ed126b6e21a39059adaa4caa6d021}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!startEchoTest@{startEchoTest}}
\index{startEchoTest@{startEchoTest}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{startEchoTest()}{startEchoTest()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::start\+Echo\+Test (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{interval\+In\+Seconds }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Starts an audio call test.

This method starts an audio call test to determine whether the audio devices (for example, headset and speaker) and the network connection are working properly.

In the audio call test, you record your voice. If the recording plays back within the set time interval, the audio devices and the network connection are working properly.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Call this method before joining a channel.
\item After calling this method, call the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ae779da1c3fe153d73e8dfb2eb59ba9e4}{stop\+Echo\+Test}} method to end the test. Otherwise, the app cannot run the next echo test, or call the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_adc937172e59bd2695ea171553a88188c}{join\+Channel}} method.
\item In the {\ttfamily L\+I\+V\+E\+\_\+\+B\+R\+O\+A\+D\+C\+A\+S\+T\+I\+NG} profile, only a host can call this method. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em interval\+In\+Seconds} & The time interval (s) between when you speak and when the recording plays back.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::enable\+Video (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Enables the video.

You can call this method either before joining a channel or during a call. If you call this method before entering a channel, the service starts the video; if you call it during a call, the audio call switches to a video call.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This method controls the underlying states of the Engine. It is still valid after one leaves the channel.
\end{DoxyNote}

\item $<$ 0\+: Failure.

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!startLastmileProbeTest@{startLastmileProbeTest}}
\index{startLastmileProbeTest@{startLastmileProbeTest}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{startLastmileProbeTest()}{startLastmileProbeTest()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::start\+Lastmile\+Probe\+Test (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_lastmile_probe_config}{Lastmile\+Probe\+Config}} \&}]{config }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Starts the last-\/mile network probe test.

This method starts the last-\/mile network probe test before joining a channel to get the uplink and downlink last-\/mile network statistics, including the bandwidth, packet loss, jitter, and round-\/trip time (R\+TT).

Call this method to check the uplink network quality before users join a channel or before an audience switches to a host. Once this method is enabled, the S\+DK returns the following callbacks\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_ac7e14d1a26eb35ef236a0662d28d2b33}{on\+Lastmile\+Quality}}\+: the S\+DK triggers this callback depending on the network conditions. This callback rates the network conditions and is more closely linked to the user experience.
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a44134dfda5d412831fa8e44fa533fca5}{on\+Lastmile\+Probe\+Result}}\+: the S\+DK triggers this callback within 30 seconds depending on the network conditions. This callback returns the real-\/time statistics of the network conditions and is more objective.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Do not call other methods before receiving the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_ac7e14d1a26eb35ef236a0662d28d2b33}{on\+Lastmile\+Quality}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a44134dfda5d412831fa8e44fa533fca5}{on\+Lastmile\+Probe\+Result}} callbacks. Otherwise, the callbacks may be interrupted.
\item In the Live-\/broadcast profile, a host should not call this method after joining a channel.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em config} & Sets the configurations of the last-\/mile network probe test. See \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_lastmile_probe_config}{Lastmile\+Probe\+Config}}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a94f3494035429684a750e1dee7ef1593}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a94f3494035429684a750e1dee7ef1593}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!stopLastmileProbeTest@{stopLastmileProbeTest}}
\index{stopLastmileProbeTest@{stopLastmileProbeTest}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{stopLastmileProbeTest()}{stopLastmileProbeTest()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::stop\+Lastmile\+Probe\+Test (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Stops the last-\/mile network probe test. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a9bcbdcee0b5c52f96b32baec1922cf2e}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a9bcbdcee0b5c52f96b32baec1922cf2e}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setVideoEncoderConfiguration@{setVideoEncoderConfiguration}}
\index{setVideoEncoderConfiguration@{setVideoEncoderConfiguration}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setVideoEncoderConfiguration()}{setVideoEncoderConfiguration()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Video\+Encoder\+Configuration (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_video_encoder_configuration}{Video\+Encoder\+Configuration}} \&}]{config }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets the video encoder configuration.

Each configuration profile corresponds to a set of video parameters, including the resolution, frame rate, and bitrate.

The parameters specified in this method are the maximum values under ideal network conditions. If the video engine cannot render the video using the specified parameters due to poor network conditions, the parameters further down the list are considered until a successful configuration is found.

{\em config} & The local video encoder configuration\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_video_encoder_configuration}{Video\+Encoder\+Configuration}}. \\

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setLowlightEnhanceOptions@{setLowlightEnhanceOptions}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setLowlightEnhanceOptions()}{setLowlightEnhanceOptions()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Lowlight\+Enhance\+Options (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{enabled,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_lowlight_enhance_options}{Lowlight\+Enhance\+Options}} \&}]{options,  }\item[{agora\+::media\+::\+M\+E\+D\+I\+A\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}]{type = {\ttfamily agora\+:\+:media\+:\+:PRIMARY\+\_\+CAMERA\+\_\+SOURCE} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets low-\/light enhancement.

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v4.\+0.\+0
\end{DoxySince}
The low-\/light enhancement feature can adaptively adjust the brightness value of the video captured in situations with low or uneven lighting, such as backlit, cloudy, or dark scenes. It restores or highlights the image details and improves the overall visual effect of the video.

You can call this method to enable the low-\/light enhancement feature and set the options of the low-\/light enhancement effect.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Before calling this method, ensure that you have integrated the following dynamic library into your project\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Android\+: {\ttfamily libagora\+\_\+segmentation\+\_\+extension.\+so}
\item i\+O\+S/mac\+OS\+: {\ttfamily Agora\+Video\+Segmentation\+Extension.\+xcframework}
\item Windows\+: {\ttfamily libagora\+\_\+segmentation\+\_\+extension.\+dll}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Call this method after \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a7d35fc62d74685d25636f04b04051958}{enable\+Video}}.
\item The low-\/light enhancement feature has certain performance requirements on devices. If your device overheats after you enable low-\/light enhancement, Agora recommends modifying the low-\/light enhancement options to a less performance-\/consuming level or disabling low-\/light enhancement entirely.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em enabled} & Sets whether to enable low-\/light enhancement\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily true}\+: Enable.
\item {\ttfamily false}\+: (Default) Disable. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em options} & The low-\/light enhancement options. See \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_lowlight_enhance_options}{Lowlight\+Enhance\+Options}}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ab1a6aabdd8a30919cca75ce27fd9f108}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ab1a6aabdd8a30919cca75ce27fd9f108}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Video\+Denoiser\+Options (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{enabled,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_video_denoiser_options}{Video\+Denoiser\+Options}} \&}]{options,  }\item[{agora\+::media\+::\+M\+E\+D\+I\+A\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}]{type = {\ttfamily agora\+:\+:media\+:\+:PRIMARY\+\_\+CAMERA\+\_\+SOURCE} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets video noise reduction.

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v4.\+0.\+0
\end{DoxySince}
Underlit environments and low-\/end video capture devices can cause video images to contain significant noise, which affects video quality. In real-\/time interactive scenarios, video noise also consumes bitstream resources and reduces encoding efficiency during encoding.

You can call this method to enable the video noise reduction feature and set the options of the video noise reduction effect.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Before calling this method, ensure that you have integrated the following dynamic library into your project\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Android\+: {\ttfamily libagora\+\_\+segmentation\+\_\+extension.\+so}
\item i\+O\+S/mac\+OS\+: {\ttfamily Agora\+Video\+Segmentation\+Extension.\+xcframework}
\item Windows\+: {\ttfamily libagora\+\_\+segmentation\+\_\+extension.\+dll}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Call this method after \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a7d35fc62d74685d25636f04b04051958}{enable\+Video}}.
\item The video noise reduction feature has certain performance requirements on devices. If your device overheats after you enable video noise reduction, Agora recommends modifying the video noise reduction options to a less performance-\/consuming level or disabling video noise reduction entirely.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em enabled} & Sets whether to enable video noise reduction\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily true}\+: Enable.
\item {\ttfamily false}\+: (Default) Disable. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em options} & The video noise reduction options. See \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_video_denoiser_options}{Video\+Denoiser\+Options}}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}

\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Color\+Enhance\+Options (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{enabled,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_color_enhance_options}{Color\+Enhance\+Options}} \&}]{options,  }\item[{agora\+::media\+::\+M\+E\+D\+I\+A\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}]{type = {\ttfamily agora\+:\+:media\+:\+:PRIMARY\+\_\+CAMERA\+\_\+SOURCE} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets color enhancement.

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v4.\+0.\+0
\end{DoxySince}
The video images captured by the camera can have color distortion. The color enhancement feature intelligently adjusts video characteristics such as saturation and contrast to enhance the video color richness and color reproduction, making the video more vivid.

You can call this method to enable the color enhancement feature and set the options of the color enhancement effect.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Before calling this method, ensure that you have integrated the following dynamic library into your project\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Android\+: {\ttfamily libagora\+\_\+segmentation\+\_\+extension.\+so}
\item i\+O\+S/mac\+OS\+: {\ttfamily Agora\+Video\+Segmentation\+Extension.\+xcframework}
\item Windows\+: {\ttfamily libagora\+\_\+segmentation\+\_\+extension.\+dll}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Call this method after \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a7d35fc62d74685d25636f04b04051958}{enable\+Video}}.
\item The color enhancement feature has certain performance requirements on devices. If your device overheats after you enable color enhancement, Agora recommends modifying the color enhancement options to a less performance-\/consuming level or disabling color enhancement entirely.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!enableVirtualBackground@{enableVirtualBackground}}
\index{enableVirtualBackground@{enableVirtualBackground}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableVirtualBackground()}{enableVirtualBackground()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::enable\+Virtual\+Background (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{enabled,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_virtual_background_source}{Virtual\+Background\+Source}}}]{background\+Source,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_segmentation_property}{Segmentation\+Property}}}]{segproperty,  }\item[{agora\+::media\+::\+M\+E\+D\+I\+A\+\_\+\+S\+O\+U\+R\+C\+E\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}]{type = {\ttfamily agora\+:\+:media\+:\+:PRIMARY\+\_\+CAMERA\+\_\+SOURCE} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Enables/\+Disables the virtual background. (beta function)

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v3.\+7.\+200
\end{DoxySince}
After enabling the virtual background function, you can replace the original background image of the local user with a custom background image. After the replacement, all users in the channel can see the custom background image.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Before calling this method, ensure that you have integrated the {\ttfamily libagora\+\_\+segmentation\+\_\+extension.\+dll} (Windows)/{\ttfamily Agora\+Video\+Segmentation\+Extension.\+framework} (mac\+OS) dynamic library into the project folder.
\item Call this method after \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a7d35fc62d74685d25636f04b04051958}{enable\+Video}}.
\item This function requires a high-\/performance device. Agora recommends that you use this function on devices with an i5 C\+PU and better.
\item Agora recommends that you use this function in scenarios that meet the following conditions\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item A high-\/definition camera device is used, and the environment is uniformly lit.
\item The captured video image is uncluttered, the user\textquotesingle{}s portrait is half-\/length and largely unobstructed, and the background is a single color that differs from the color of the user\textquotesingle{}s clothing.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em enabled} & Sets whether to enable the virtual background\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: Enable.
\item false\+: Disable. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em background\+Source} & The custom background image. See \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_virtual_background_source}{Virtual\+Background\+Source}}. {\bfseries{Note}}\+: To adapt the resolution of the custom background image to the resolution of the S\+DK capturing video, the S\+DK scales and crops the custom background image while ensuring that the content of the custom background image is not distorted.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac3b3f8c3bd296491d71d9eddb79d6649}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac3b3f8c3bd296491d71d9eddb79d6649}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!enableRemoteSuperResolution@{enableRemoteSuperResolution}}
\index{enableRemoteSuperResolution@{enableRemoteSuperResolution}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableRemoteSuperResolution()}{enableRemoteSuperResolution()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::enable\+Remote\+Super\+Resolution (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uid\+\_\+t}]{user\+Id,  }\item[{bool}]{enable }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Enables/\+Disables the super resolution feature for a remote user\textquotesingle{}s video. (beta feature)

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
v4.\+0.\+0
\end{DoxySince}
This feature effectively boosts the resolution of a remote user\textquotesingle{}s video seen by the local user. If the original resolution of a remote user\textquotesingle{}s video is a  b, the local user\textquotesingle{}s device can render the remote video at a resolution of 2a  2b after you enable this feature.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
The super resolution feature requires extra system resources. To balance the visual experience and system consumption, the S\+DK poses the following restrictions\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This feature can only be enabled for a single remote user.
\item The original resolution of the remote user\textquotesingle{}s video cannot exceed a certain range. If the local user use super resolution on Android, the original resolution of the remote user\textquotesingle{}s video cannot exceed 640  360 pixels; if the local user use super resolution on i\+OS, the original resolution of the remote user\textquotesingle{}s video cannot exceed 640  480 pixels.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item This method is for Android and i\+OS only.
\item Before calling this method, ensure that you have integrated the following dynamic library into your project\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Android\+: {\ttfamily libagora\+\_\+super\+\_\+resolution\+\_\+extension.\+so}
\item i\+OS\+: {\ttfamily Agora\+Super\+Resolution\+Extension.\+xcframework}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Because this method has certain system performance requirements, Agora recommends that you use the following devices or better\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Android\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item V\+I\+VO\+: V1821A, N\+EX S, 1914A, 1916A, 1962A, 1824BA, X60, X60 Pro
\item O\+P\+PO\+: P\+C\+C\+M00, Find X3
\item One\+Plus\+: A6000
\item Xiaomi\+: Mi 8, Mi 9, Mi 10, Mi 11, M\+I\+X3, Redmi K20 Pro
\item S\+A\+M\+S\+U\+NG\+: S\+M-\/\+G9600, S\+M-\/\+G9650, S\+M-\/\+N9600, S\+M-\/\+G9708, S\+M-\/\+G960U, S\+M-\/\+G9750, S20, S21
\item H\+U\+A\+W\+EI\+: S\+E\+A-\/\+A\+L00, E\+L\+E-\/\+A\+L00, V\+O\+G-\/\+A\+L00, Y\+A\+L-\/\+A\+L10, H\+M\+A-\/\+A\+L00, E\+V\+R-\/\+A\+N00, nova 4, nova 5 Pro, nova 6 5G, nova 7 5G, Mate 30, Mate 30 Pro, Mate 40, Mate 40 Pro, P40 P40 Pro, H\+U\+A\+W\+EI Media\+Pad M6, Mate\+Pad 10.\+8
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item i\+OS (i\+OS 12.\+0 or later)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item i\+Phone XR
\item i\+Phone XS
\item i\+Phone XS Max
\item i\+Phone 11
\item i\+Phone 11 Pro
\item i\+Phone 11 Pro Max
\item i\+Phone 12
\item i\+Phone 12 mini
\item i\+Phone 12 Pro
\item i\+Phone 12 Pro Max
\item i\+Phone 12 SE (2nd generation)
\item i\+Pad Pro 11-\/inch (3rd generation)
\item i\+Pad Pro 12.\+9-\/inch (3rd generation)
\item i\+Pad Air (3rd generation)
\item i\+Pad Air (4th generation)
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac166814787b0a1d8da5f5c632dd7cdcf}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac166814787b0a1d8da5f5c632dd7cdcf}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setupRemoteVideo@{setupRemoteVideo}}
\index{setupRemoteVideo@{setupRemoteVideo}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setupRemoteVideo()}{setupRemoteVideo()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::setup\+Remote\+Video (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_video_canvas}{Video\+Canvas}} \&}]{canvas }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Initializes the video view of a remote user.

This method initializes the video view of a remote stream on the local device. It affects only the video view that the local user sees.

Usually the app should specify the {\ttfamily uid} of the remote video in the method call before the remote user joins the channel. If the remote {\ttfamily uid} is unknown to the app, set it later when the app receives the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_a985a675469baf9d54feb8781732e0ca8}{on\+User\+Joined}} callback.

To unbind the remote user from the view, set {\ttfamily view} in \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_video_canvas}{Video\+Canvas}} as {\ttfamily null}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Ensure that you call this method in the UI thread.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em canvas} & The remote video view settings\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_video_canvas}{Video\+Canvas}}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}

Initializes the local video view.

This method initializes the video view of the local stream on the local device. It affects only the video view that the local user sees, not the published local video stream.

To unbind the local video from the view, set {\ttfamily view} in \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_video_canvas}{Video\+Canvas}} as {\ttfamily null}.

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!enableLocalAudio@{enableLocalAudio}}
\index{enableLocalAudio@{enableLocalAudio}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableLocalAudio()}{enableLocalAudio()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::enable\+Local\+Audio (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Enables or disables the local audio capture.

The audio function is enabled by default. This method disables or re-\/enables the local audio function, that is, to stop or restart local audio capture and processing.

This method does not affect receiving or playing the remote audio streams, and {\ttfamily enable\+Local\+Audio} (false) is applicable to scenarios where the user wants to receive remote audio streams without sending any audio stream to other users in the channel.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em enabled} & Determines whether to disable or re-\/enable the local audio function\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: (Default) Re-\/enable the local audio function, that is, to start local audio capture and processing.
\item false\+: Disable the local audio function, that is, to stop local audio capture and processing.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a08a34d5b85a225390a18467c92a7b6f9}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a08a34d5b85a225390a18467c92a7b6f9}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!muteLocalAudioStream@{muteLocalAudioStream}}
\index{muteLocalAudioStream@{muteLocalAudioStream}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{muteLocalAudioStream()}{muteLocalAudioStream()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::mute\+Local\+Audio\+Stream (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{mute }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Stops or resumes sending the local audio stream.

After calling this method successfully, the S\+DK triggers the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_aa168380f86f1dc2df1c269a785c56612}{on\+Remote\+Audio\+State\+Changed}} callback with the following parameters\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item R\+E\+M\+O\+T\+E\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+S\+T\+O\+P\+P\+E\+D(0) and R\+E\+M\+O\+T\+E\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+O\+N\+\_\+\+R\+E\+M\+O\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+U\+T\+E\+D(5).
\item R\+E\+M\+O\+T\+E\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+C\+O\+D\+I\+N\+G(2) and R\+E\+M\+O\+T\+E\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+R\+E\+A\+S\+O\+N\+\_\+\+R\+E\+M\+O\+T\+E\+\_\+\+U\+N\+M\+U\+T\+E\+D(6).
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item When {\ttfamily mute} is set as {\ttfamily true}, this method does not disable the microphone, which does not affect any ongoing recording.
\item If you call \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_aab53788c74da25080bad61f0525d12ae}{set\+Channel\+Profile}} after this method, the S\+DK resets whether or not to mute the local audio according to the channel profile and user role. Therefore, we recommend calling this method after the {\ttfamily set\+Channel\+Profile} method.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mute} & Determines whether to send or stop sending the local audio stream\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: Stop sending the local audio stream.
\item false\+: (Default) Send the local audio stream.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac061a3c81eba2d203a7511e59466e6a0}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac061a3c81eba2d203a7511e59466e6a0}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!muteAllRemoteAudioStreams@{muteAllRemoteAudioStreams}}
\index{muteAllRemoteAudioStreams@{muteAllRemoteAudioStreams}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{muteAllRemoteAudioStreams()}{muteAllRemoteAudioStreams()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{mute }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Stops or resumes receiving all remote audio stream.

This method works for all remote users that join or will join a channel using the {\ttfamily join\+Channel} method. It is equivalent to the {\ttfamily auto\+Subscribe\+Audio} member in the \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_channel_media_options}{Channel\+Media\+Options}} class. You can call this method before, during, or after a call.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If you call mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams(true) before joining a channel, the local user does not receive any audio stream after joining the channel.
\item If you call mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams(true) after joining a channel, the local use stops receiving any audio stream from any user in the channel, including any user who joins the channel after you call this method.
\item If you call mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams(true) after leaving a channel, the local user does not receive any audio stream the next time the user joins a channel.
\end{DoxyItemize}

After you successfully call mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams(true), you can take the following actions\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item To resume receiving all remote audio streams, call mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams(false).
\item To resume receiving the audio stream of a specified user, call mute\+Remote\+Audio\+Stream(uid, false), where uid is the ID of the user whose audio stream you want to resume receiving.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The result of calling this method is affected by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a996401c7ba33c6ec59527c5d109f548f}{enable\+Audio}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a1929f01411e983ed776275fe8e8ad45e}{disable\+Audio}}. Settings in mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams stop taking effect if either of the following occurs\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Calling {\ttfamily enable\+Audio} after mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams(true).
\item Calling {\ttfamily disable\+Audio} after mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams(false).
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item This method only works for the channel created by calling {\ttfamily join\+Channel}. To set whether to receive remote audio streams for a specific channel, Agora recommends using {\ttfamily auto\+Subscribe\+Audio} in the \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_channel_media_options}{Channel\+Media\+Options}} class. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mute} & Whether to stop receiving remote audio streams\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: Stop receiving any remote audio stream.
\item false\+: (Default) Resume receiving all remote audio streams. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a2a865bf8830c9ab8b600fa01d61fb4ab}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a2a865bf8830c9ab8b600fa01d61fb4ab}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setDefaultMuteAllRemoteAudioStreams()}{setDefaultMuteAllRemoteAudioStreams()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Default\+Mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{mute }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Determines whether to receive all remote audio streams by default.

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000014}{Deprecated}}]This method is deprecated. To set whether to receive remote audio streams by default, call \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac061a3c81eba2d203a7511e59466e6a0}{mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams}} before calling {\ttfamily join\+Channel}\end{DoxyRefDesc}


Use this method to set whether to receive audio streams of subsequent peer users. Agora recommends calling it before joining a channel.

A successful call of set\+Default\+Mute\+All\+Remote\+Audio\+Streams(true) results in that the local user not receiving any audio stream after joining a channel.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: Do not receive any remote audio stream by default.
\item false\+: (Default) Receive remote audio streams by default.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyItemize}

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!muteRemoteAudioStream@{muteRemoteAudioStream}}

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!enableLocalVideo@{enableLocalVideo}}
\index{enableLocalVideo@{enableLocalVideo}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableLocalVideo()}{enableLocalVideo()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::enable\+Local\+Video (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Disables or re-\/enables the local video capture.

Once you enable the video using \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a7d35fc62d74685d25636f04b04051958}{enable\+Video}}, the local video is enabled by default. This method disables or re-\/enables the local video capture.

{\ttfamily enable\+Local\+Video(false)} applies to scenarios when the user wants to watch the remote video without sending any video stream to the other user.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Call this method after {\ttfamily enable\+Video}. Otherwise, this method may not work properly.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em enabled} & Determines whether to disable or re-\/enable the local video, including the capturer, renderer, and sender\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: (Default) Re-\/enable the local video.
\item false\+: Disable the local video. Once the local video is disabled, the remote users can no longer receive the video stream of this user, while this user can still receive the video streams of other remote users. When you set {\ttfamily enabled} as {\ttfamily false}, this method does not require a local camera.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a897a09788641f26252be642bb7045ee4}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a897a09788641f26252be642bb7045ee4}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!muteAllRemoteVideoStreams@{muteAllRemoteVideoStreams}}
\index{muteAllRemoteVideoStreams@{muteAllRemoteVideoStreams}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{muteAllRemoteVideoStreams()}{muteAllRemoteVideoStreams()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{mute }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Stops or resumes receiving all remote video streams.

This method works for all remote users that join or will join a channel using the {\ttfamily join\+Channel} method. It is equivalent to the {\ttfamily auto\+Subscribe\+Video} member in the \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_channel_media_options}{Channel\+Media\+Options}} class. You can call this method before, during, or after a call.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If you call mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams(true) before joining a channel, the local user does not receive any video stream after joining the channel.
\item If you call mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams(true) after joining a channel, the local use stops receiving any video stream from any user in the channel, including any user who joins the channel after you call this method.
\item If you call mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams(true) after leaving a channel, the local user does not receive any video stream the next time the user joins a channel.
\end{DoxyItemize}

After you successfully call mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams(true), you can take the following actions\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item To resume receiving all remote video streams, call mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams(false).
\item To resume receiving the video stream of a specified user, call mute\+Remote\+Video\+Stream(uid, false), where uid is the ID of the user whose video stream you want to resume receiving.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The result of calling this method is affected by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a7d35fc62d74685d25636f04b04051958}{enable\+Video}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ac8eca0135b3ab7cecb84e2b81b89a85d}{disable\+Video}}. Settings in mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams stop taking effect if either of the following occurs\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Calling {\ttfamily enable\+Video} after mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams(true).
\item Calling {\ttfamily disable\+Video} after mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams(false).
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item This method only works for the channel created by calling {\ttfamily join\+Channel}. To set whether to receive remote audio streams for a specific channel, Agora recommends using {\ttfamily auto\+Subscribe\+Video} in the \mbox{\hyperlink{structagora_1_1rtc_1_1_channel_media_options}{Channel\+Media\+Options}} class. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mute} & Whether to stop receiving remote video streams\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: Stop receiving any remote video stream.
\item false\+: (Default) Resume receiving all remote video streams. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_af18d93c630d863bd7b5bb697aac82626}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_af18d93c630d863bd7b5bb697aac82626}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setDefaultMuteAllRemoteVideoStreams@{setDefaultMuteAllRemoteVideoStreams}}
\index{setDefaultMuteAllRemoteVideoStreams@{setDefaultMuteAllRemoteVideoStreams}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setDefaultMuteAllRemoteVideoStreams()}{setDefaultMuteAllRemoteVideoStreams()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Default\+Mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{mute }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Determines whether to receive all remote video streams by default.

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000015}{Deprecated}}]This method is deprecated. To set whether to receive remote video streams by default, call \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a897a09788641f26252be642bb7045ee4}{mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams}} before calling {\ttfamily join\+Channel}.\end{DoxyRefDesc}


Use this method to set whether to receive video streams of subsequent peer users. Agora recommends calling it before joining a channel.

A successful call of set\+Default\+Mute\+All\+Remote\+Video\+Streams(true) results in that the local user not receiving any video stream after joining a channel.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mute} & Whether to receive remote video streams by default\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: Do not receive any remote video stream by default.
\item false\+: (Default) Receive remote video streams by default. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
int
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::mute\+Remote\+Video\+Stream (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uid\+\_\+t}]{uid,  }\item[{bool}]{mute }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Stops or resumes receiving the video stream of a specified user.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
You can call this method before or after joining a channel. If a user leaves a channel, the settings in this method become invalid.
\end{DoxyNote}

\hline
{\em mute} & Whether to stop receiving the video stream of the specified user\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: Stop receiving the video stream of the specified user.
\item false\+: (Default) Resume receiving the video stream of the specified user.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline

\begin{DoxyItemize}

Sets the remote video stream type.

If the remote user has enabled the dual-\/stream mode, by default the S\+DK receives the high-\/stream video by Call this method to switch to the low-\/stream video.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableAudioVolumeIndication()}{enableAudioVolumeIndication()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::enable\+Audio\+Volume\+Indication (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{interval,  }\item[{int}]{smooth,  }\item[{bool}]{report\+Vad }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Enables the {\ttfamily on\+Audio\+Volume\+Indication} callback to report on which users are speaking and the speakers\textquotesingle{} volume.

Once the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_aab1184a2b276f509870c055a9ff8fac4}{on\+Audio\+Volume\+Indication}} callback is enabled, the S\+DK returns the volume indication in the at the time interval set in {\ttfamily enable\+Audio\+Volume\+Indication}, regardless of whether any user is speaking in the channel.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em interval} & Sets the time interval between two consecutive volume indications\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item $<$= 0\+: Disables the volume indication.
\item $>$ 0\+: Time interval (ms) between two consecutive volume indications, and should be integral multiple of 200 (less than 200 will be set to 200). 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em smooth} & The smoothing factor that sets the sensitivity of the audio volume indicator. The value range is \mbox{[}0, 10\mbox{]}. The greater the value, the more sensitive the indicator. The recommended value is 3.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{startAudioRecording()}{startAudioRecording()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::start\+Audio\+Recording (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{file\+Path,  }\item[{A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+R\+E\+C\+O\+R\+D\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}]{quality }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Starts an audio recording.

The S\+DK allows recording during a call, which supports either one of the following two formats\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item .wav\+: Large file size with high sound fidelity
\item .aac\+: Small file size with low sound fidelity
\end{DoxyItemize}

Ensure that the directory to save the recording file exists and is writable. This method is usually called after the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_adc937172e59bd2695ea171553a88188c}{join\+Channel()}} method. The recording automatically stops when the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a51c12d209373650638bfd82e28777081}{leave\+Channel()}} method is called.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em file\+Path} & Full file path of the recording file. The string of the file name is in U\+T\+F-\/8 code. \\
\hline
{\em quality} & Sets the audio recording quality\+: \#\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+R\+E\+C\+O\+R\+D\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+L\+I\+T\+Y\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_adb392026425663e5b9f90fe90130e5a5}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_adb392026425663e5b9f90fe90130e5a5}}

The recording automatically stops when the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a51c12d209373650638bfd82e28777081}{leave\+Channel()}} method is called.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a8739ebb08c6d97c1ee708889ef834d5f}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a8739ebb08c6d97c1ee708889ef834d5f}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!startAudioMixing@{startAudioMixing}}
\index{startAudioMixing@{startAudioMixing}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{startAudioMixing()}{startAudioMixing()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::start\+Audio\+Mixing (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{file\+Path,  }\item[{bool}]{loopback,  }\item[{int}]{cycle }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Starts playing and mixing the music file.

This method mixes the specified local audio file with the audio stream from the microphone. You can choose whether the other user can hear the local audio playback and specify the number of playback loops. This method also supports online music playback.

After calling this method successfully, the S\+DK triggers the

\mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_ae2e257d7bbf120b970b600b9b3731a07}{on\+Audio\+Mixing\+State\+Changed}} (P\+L\+AY) callback on the local client. When the audio mixing file playback finishes after calling this method, the S\+DK triggers the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_ae2e257d7bbf120b970b600b9b3731a07}{on\+Audio\+Mixing\+State\+Changed}} (S\+T\+O\+P\+P\+ED) callback on the local client.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Call this method after joining a channel, otherwise issues may occur.
\item If the local audio mixing file does not exist, or if the S\+DK does not support the file format or cannot access the music file U\+RL, the S\+DK returns \#\+W\+A\+R\+N\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+N\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR (701).
\item If you want to play an online music file, ensure that the time interval between calling this method is more than 100 ms, or the {\ttfamily A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+\+T\+O\+O\+\_\+\+F\+R\+E\+Q\+U\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+C\+A\+L\+L(702)} error code occurs.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em file\+Path} & Pointer to the absolute path (including the suffixes of the filename) of the local or online audio file to mix, for example, c\+:/music/au dio.\+mp4. Supported audio formats\+: 3GP, A\+SF, A\+D\+TS, A\+VI, M\+P3, M\+P4, M\+P\+E\+G-\/4, S\+A\+MI, and W\+A\+VE. \\
\hline
{\em loopback} & Sets which user can hear the audio mixing\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: Only the local user can hear the audio mixing.
\item false\+: Both users can hear the audio mixing.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em cycle} & Sets the number of playback loops\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Positive integer\+: Number of playback loops.
\item {\ttfamily -\/1}\+: Infinite playback loops.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a88a90b9433ec193f9821738ba55e6ec3}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a88a90b9433ec193f9821738ba55e6ec3}}

\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setAudioMixingDualMonoMode@{setAudioMixingDualMonoMode}}
\index{setAudioMixingDualMonoMode@{setAudioMixingDualMonoMode}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setAudioMixingDualMonoMode()}{setAudioMixingDualMonoMode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Audio\+Mixing\+Dual\+Mono\+Mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{media\+::\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+D\+U\+A\+L\+\_\+\+M\+O\+N\+O\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE}]{mode }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

In dual-\/channel music files, different audio data can be stored on the left and right channels. According to actual needs, you can set the channel mode as the original mode, the left channel mode, the right channel mode or the mixed mode


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mode} & The mode of channel mode\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a26b117f7e097801b03522f7da9257425}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a26b117f7e097801b03522f7da9257425}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!setAudioMixingPitch@{setAudioMixingPitch}}
\index{setAudioMixingPitch@{setAudioMixingPitch}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setAudioMixingPitch()}{setAudioMixingPitch()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::set\+Audio\+Mixing\+Pitch (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{pitch }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Sets the pitch of the local music file.

When a local music file is mixed with a local human voice, call this method to set the pitch of the local music file only.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Call this method after calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a8739ebb08c6d97c1ee708889ef834d5f}{start\+Audio\+Mixing}} and receiving the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_event_handler_ae2e257d7bbf120b970b600b9b3731a07}{on\+Audio\+Mixing\+State\+Changed}} (A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+L\+A\+Y\+I\+NG) callback.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em pitch} & Sets the pitch of the local music file by chromatic scale. The default value is 0, which means keeping the original pitch. The value ranges from -\/12 to 12, and the pitch value between consecutive values is a chromatic value. The greater the absolute value of this parameter, the higher or lower the pitch of the local music file.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a0e9787c57db5b5e8fcc53ef5bb6d24c7}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a0e9787c57db5b5e8fcc53ef5bb6d24c7}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_add9a7fd856700acd288d47ff3c7da19d}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_add9a7fd856700acd288d47ff3c7da19d}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a075dd8a712ecd5f610004ca1bc089d4b}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a075dd8a712ecd5f610004ca1bc089d4b}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!preloadEffect@{preloadEffect}}
\index{preloadEffect@{preloadEffect}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{preloadEffect()}{preloadEffect()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::preload\+Effect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{sound\+Id,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{file\+Path,  }\item[{int}]{start\+Pos = {\ttfamily 0} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Preloads a specified audio effect.

This method preloads only one specified audio effect into the memory each time it is called. To preload multiple audio effects, call this method multiple times.

After preloading, you can call \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a49de4c18c3fbac4a5e905cd0e0243557}{play\+Effect}} to play the preloaded audio effect or call \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_aba9b070620c7e7659841dd6f94331941}{play\+All\+Effects}} to play all the preloaded audio effects.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item To ensure smooth communication, limit the size of the audio effect file.
\item Agora recommends calling this method before joining the channel.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sound\+Id} & The ID of the audio effect. \\
\hline
{\em file\+Path} & The absolute path of the local audio effect file or the U\+RL of the online audio effect file. Supported audio formats\+: mp3, mp4, m4a, aac, 3gp, mkv, and wav.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a49de4c18c3fbac4a5e905cd0e0243557}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a49de4c18c3fbac4a5e905cd0e0243557}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!playEffect@{playEffect}}
\index{playEffect@{playEffect}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{playEffect()}{playEffect()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::play\+Effect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{sound\+Id,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{file\+Path,  }\item[{int}]{loop\+Count,  }\item[{double}]{pitch,  }\item[{double}]{pan,  }\item[{int}]{gain,  }\item[{bool}]{publish = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{int}]{start\+Pos = {\ttfamily 0} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Plays a specified audio effect.

After calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a075dd8a712ecd5f610004ca1bc089d4b}{preload\+Effect}}, you can call this method to play the specified audio effect for all users in the channel.

This method plays only one specified audio effect each time it is called. To play multiple audio effects, call this method multiple times.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Agora recommends playing no more than three audio effects at the same time.
\item The ID and file path of the audio effect in this method must be the same as that in the \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a075dd8a712ecd5f610004ca1bc089d4b}{preload\+Effect}} method.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sound\+Id} & The ID of the audio effect. \\
\hline
{\em file\+Path} & The absolute path of the local audio effect file or the U\+RL of the online audio effect file. Supported audio formats\+: mp3, mp4, m4a, aac, 3gp, mkv, and wav. \\
\hline
{\em loop\+Count} & The number of times the audio effect loops\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily -\/1}\+: Play the audio effect in an indefinite loop until \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ad74eb7c7799b8762bff2b1e7e7bba8b9}{stop\+Effect}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a888ecfec4fda81831988898420d60e49}{stop\+All\+Effects}}
\item {\ttfamily 0}\+: Play the audio effect once.
\item {\ttfamily 1}\+: Play the audio effect twice. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em pitch} & The pitch of the audio effect. The value ranges between 0.\+5 and 2.\+0. The default value is {\ttfamily 1.\+0} (original pitch). The lower the value, the lower the pitch. \\
\hline
{\em pan} & The spatial position of the audio effect. The value ranges between -\/1.\+0 and 1.\+0\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily -\/1.\+0}\+: The audio effect displays to the left.
\item {\ttfamily 0.\+0}\+: The audio effect displays ahead.
\item {\ttfamily 1.\+0}\+: The audio effect displays to the right. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em gain} & The volume of the audio effect. The value ranges between 0 and 100. The default value is {\ttfamily 100} (original volume). The lower the value, the lower the volume of the audio effect. \\
\hline
{\em publish} & Sets whether to publish the audio effect to the remote\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: Publish the audio effect to the remote.
\item false\+: (Default) Do not publish the audio effect to the remote.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_aba9b070620c7e7659841dd6f94331941}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_aba9b070620c7e7659841dd6f94331941}} 
\index{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}!playAllEffects@{playAllEffects}}
\index{playAllEffects@{playAllEffects}!agora::rtc::IRtcEngine@{agora::rtc::IRtcEngine}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{playAllEffects()}{playAllEffects()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual int agora\+::rtc\+::\+I\+Rtc\+Engine\+::play\+All\+Effects (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{loop\+Count,  }\item[{double}]{pitch,  }\item[{double}]{pan,  }\item[{int}]{gain,  }\item[{bool}]{publish = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [pure virtual]}}

Plays all audio effects.

After calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a075dd8a712ecd5f610004ca1bc089d4b}{preload\+Effect}} multiple times to preload multiple audio effects into the memory, you can call this method to play all the specified audio effects for all users in the channel.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em loop\+Count} & The number of times the audio effect loops\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily -\/1}\+: Play the audio effect in an indefinite loop until \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ad74eb7c7799b8762bff2b1e7e7bba8b9}{stop\+Effect}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_a888ecfec4fda81831988898420d60e49}{stop\+All\+Effects}}
\item {\ttfamily 0}\+: Play the audio effect once.
\item {\ttfamily 1}\+: Play the audio effect twice. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em pitch} & The pitch of the audio effect. The value ranges between 0.\+5 and 2.\+0. The default value is {\ttfamily 1.\+0} (original pitch). The lower the value, the lower the pitch. \\
\hline
{\em pan} & The spatial position of the audio effect. The value ranges between -\/1.\+0 and 1.\+0\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily -\/1.\+0}\+: The audio effect displays to the left.
\item {\ttfamily 0.\+0}\+: The audio effect displays ahead.
\item {\ttfamily 1.\+0}\+: The audio effect displays to the right. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
{\em gain} & The volume of the audio effect. The value ranges between 0 and 100. The default value is {\ttfamily 100} (original volume). The lower the value, the lower the volume of the audio effect. \\
\hline
{\em publish} & Sets whether to publish the audio effect to the remote\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item true\+: Publish the audio effect to the remote.
\item false\+: (Default) Do not publish the audio effect to the remote.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: Success.
\item $<$ 0\+: Failure. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ab53220e4d12755dc17410531d2b2eebb}\label{classagora_1_1rtc_1_1_i_rtc_engine_ab53220e4d12755dc17410531d2b2eebb}}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Call this method after joining a channel.
\item For the audio file formats supported by this method, see \href{https://docs.agora.io/en/faq/audio_format}{\texttt{ What formats of audio files does the Agora R\+TC S\+DK support}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em file\+Path} & The absolute path or U\+RL address (including the filename extensions) of the music file. For example\+: {\ttfamily C\+:\textbackslash{}music\textbackslash{}audio.\+mp4}. When you access a local file on Android, Agora recommends passing a U\+RI address or the path starts with {\ttfamily /assets/} in this parameter.\\
\hline
